***вооружаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вооружаться.html>вооружа́ться</a> (31321)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вооружа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vooružátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружаться.html>вооружа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vooružátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружиться.html>вооружи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to arm, to provide, to furnish <i>(oneself)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружаться.html>вооружа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зубо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vooružátʹsja</b> do zubóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be armed to the teeth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружаться.html>вооружа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:терпение.html>терпе́нием</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vooružátʹsja</b> terpénijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to arm oneself with patience, to be patient, to have patience</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вооружа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vooružátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружение.html>вооруже́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vooružénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вооружившийся.html>вооружи́вшийся</a> (14677)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружившийся.html>вооружи́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vooružívšijsja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружиться.html>вооружи́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vooružítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: armed <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">equipped, especially with a weapon</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:житель.html>жи́тель</a> санкт-петербу́рга, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружившийся.html>вооружи́вшийся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистоле́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глушитель.html>глуши́телем</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:получить.html>получи́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Žítelʹ Sankt-Peterbúrga, <b>vooružívšijsja</b> pistolétom s glušítelem, polučíl pjatʹ let.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The resident of St. Petersburg <b>who was armed</b> with a pistol with a silencer received five years.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вооружить.html>вооружи́ть</a> (24460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружить.html>вооружи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vooružítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вооружа́ть</b>)

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вооружить.html>вооружи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vooružítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***воочию.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воочию.html>воо́чию</a> (16430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въ очью</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭ očĭju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, consisting of the locative dual of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>око</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oko</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eye</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воочию.html>воо́чию</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voóčiju</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary or dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> with one's own eyes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воочию.html>воо́чию</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:убедиться.html>убеди́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voóčiju</b> ubedítʹsja v čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to see smth with one's own eyes; see smth for oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>plainly, clearly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воочию.html>воо́чию</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:представить.html>предста́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voóčiju</b> predstávitʹ sebé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">clearly imagine smth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вопивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопивший.html>вопи́вший</a> (6086)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***вопить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопить.html>вопи́ть</a> (6086)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">въпити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭpiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shriek, yell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вопить.html>вопи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vopítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завопить.html>завопи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to yell, to scream, to howl</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вопия́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vopijátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орать.html>ора́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">orátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выть.html>выть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реветь.html>реве́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">revétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">во-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плоть.html>плоть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plotʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воплотить.html>воплоти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voplotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***воплощать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воплощать.html>воплоща́ть</a> (20507)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воплотить.html>воплоти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voplotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воплощать.html>воплоща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voploščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воплотить.html>воплоти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to incarnate, to embody, to personify</li>
<li>to realize (a dream, a project, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воплощать.html>воплоща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voploščátʹ</b> v žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a reality</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воплощаться.html>воплоща́ться</a> (24336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воплощать.html>воплоща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voploščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воплощаться.html>воплоща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voploščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воплотиться.html>воплоти́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be incarnated/embodied <i>(in, by)</i></li>
<li>to ro be personified <i>(by)</i></li>
<li>to be realized/implemented, to be put into action/practice, to come true</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воплощать.html>воплоща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voploščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воплощение.html>воплоще́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">voploščénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***вопреки.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопреки.html>вопреки́</a> (4688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въпрѣкы</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭprěky</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*реr-kъ</i>, whose first element comes from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*preh₂-</i> and is thus cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">for</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вопреки.html>вопреки́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voprekí</span>) <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">+ dative case</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>in spite of, contrary to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вопреки.html>вопреки́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:распространённый.html>распространённому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мнение.html>мне́нию</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чшие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ресторан.html>рестора́ны</a> Франции <a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>нахо́дятся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вовсе.html>во́все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> Париже</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voprekí</b> rasprostranjónnomu mnéniju, lúčšije restorány Francii naxódjatsja vóvse ne v Pariže</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>contrary to</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> belief, the best French restaurants are nowhere around Paris</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:судья.html>судьи</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вопреки.html>вопреки́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прогноз.html>прогно́зам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скептик.html>ске́птиков</a>, префере́нций <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́евам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лали</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sudʹi, <b>voprekí</b> prognózam sképtikov, preferéncij xozjájevam ne délali</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">judges, <b>in spite</b> of the skeptics' forecast, did not favour the owner</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>вор</a> (2198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:врать.html>врать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vratʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lie</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>вор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>во́ра</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>вора́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>во́ры</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>воры́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>воро́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воровка.html>воро́вка</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Nonstandard but common.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>thief</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> traitor, apostate, outlaw</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Clipping of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>вор</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vor v zakóne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">thief</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тать.html>тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похититель.html>похити́тель</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poxitítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***ворваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ворваться.html>ворва́ться</a> (4479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">во-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ворваться.html>ворва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vorvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:врываться.html>врыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rush into, to burst, to enter by force, to violently or hurriedly, to intrude</li></ol>
